"nerves head, open approach. this class includes one or more of 22 standard surgical interventions or procedures on component parts of the nerves of the head, open approach.  these surgical interventions or procedures are listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems or icd-10 pcs under code 01.. . "
"nerves head, open approach. this class includes one or more of 22 standard surgical interventions or procedures on component parts of the nerves of the head, open approach.  these surgical interventions or procedures are listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems or icd-10 pcs under code 01.. destruction of head and neck sympathetic nerve,  open approach. this classification denotes the group of activities that yields a surgical intervention or procedure to destruction of head and neck sympathetic nerve,  open approach.this surgical intervention or procedure is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems or icd-10 as code 015k0zz. "
